1

GENERAL INFORMATION

Aligarh Muslim University (AMU) is one of the oldest premier Central Universities of India with a

unique and rich culture of its own. It owes its existence to the selfless and untiring efforts of the great

visionary SIR SYED AHMAD KHAN. Deeply moved by the socio-economic and educational plight of

his community after the First War of Independence of 1857, he was quick to realize that the panacea

for these ills lay in inculcating the spirit of free enquiry and modernism in the community.His
exposure to the British Universities, particularly those at Oxford and Cambridge, and their public

schools, inspired him with a new vision of a harmonious pattern of culture, combining the best

elements in the cultures of the East with the arts and sciences of the West. In 1875 he founded a

High School at Aligarh, which, within three years, was raised to a College known as Mohammadan
Anglo Oriental College which metamorphosed into Aligarh Muslim University in 1920 through an Act

of Parliament.

Due attention was also paid to the education of girls. In 1942 the Muslim Girls’ School was raised to

the status of a full-fledged Degree College for Women. Since 1951 it is one of the several institutions

maintained by Aligarh Muslim University. Undergraduate women students in the Faculties of
Agricultural Sciences, Arts, Commerce, Life Sciences, Science, Social Sciences and Theology

receive instructions in the Women’s College.

In tune with the ideals of Sir Syed Ahmad Khan and with the aim to impart quality education to a

larger section of the community, Aligarh Muslim University proposed opening of AMU Centres at

different locations throughout the country. The proposed Centres were envisaged to grow and be

replicas of the University. In the year 2010, AMU Centre at Malappuram, Kerala and AMU Centre at
Murshidabad, West Bengal came into existence with students being admitted to courses in Law and

Management. In the year 2013, AMU Centre at Kishanganj, Bihar was also established and B.Ed.

programme was started at all three Centres.

Aligarh is situated in the middle of Doab – the land between the Ganga and Yamuna rivers, at a

distance of 130 km Southeast of Delhi on the Delhi-Howrah rail route and the Grand Trunk Road.

The latitude is 27

```
o
54' N and longitude is 78
```
```
o
05' E. The climate is hot and dry in summer and cold
```
and dry in winter with an intervening rainy season. The University campus is 2 kms away from the
Aligarh Railway Station.

Malappuram is the headquarters of the district of the same name in the state of Kerala. It literally

means `a land on top hills’ and is situated 50 km southeast of Kozhikode, bounded by the Nilgiri hills

in the east, the Arabian Sea in the west and Thrissur and Palakkad districts in the South. The

Malappuram district extends from 10o and 12^ o N latitudes and 75^ o to 77^ o longitudes. The climate is

generally hot and humid with the annual range of temperature varying between 20^ oC and 30^ oC.

Murshidabad district got its present name from the Nawab Murshid Quli Khan who made

Murshidabad the capital city of Suba Bangla, comprising the Bengal, Bihar and Orissa. The district

of Murshidabad is situated to the south of the Ganga River in West Bengal. It extends from 23o 43’
to 24o 52’ N latitudes, and 87o 49’ to 88o 44’ E longitudes. Murshidabad has a tropical wet and dry

climate and the monthly mean temperature varies from 17 oC to 35 oC.

Kishanganj was initially known as Nepalgarh. During Mughal period its name got converted to
Alamganj which was subsequently renamed as Kishanganj. Kishanganj district was carved out of

Purnea in 1990. It is located between 25o 20’ and 26o 30’ N latitudes, and 87o 7’ and 88o 19’ E

longitudes. The temperature varies between 5^0 C to 41^0 C with an average temperature of 27^0 C

FACULTIES / INSTITUTIONS

Aligarh Muslim University (AMU) draws students from all corners of the country as well as foreign

countries, especially Africa, West Asia and Southeast Asia.


2

The University has 1 3 Faculties viz. Agricultural Sciences  Arts  Commerce  Engineering
& Technology  International Studies Law Life Sciences Medicine Management Studies

& Research  Science Social Sciences Theology Unani Medicine, each comprising of

several Departments of Studies.

The University also maintains a number of Colleges, Institutes, Centres and Schools. Notably among
them are Women’s College Zakir Hussain College of Engineering & Technology Ajmal Khan

Tibbiya College Jawaharlal Nehru Medical College Dr. Ziauddin Ahmad Dental College

College of Nursing Para Medical College Community College  University Polytechnic

Women’s Polytechnic Centre for Promotion of Educational and Cultural Advancement of

Muslims of India (CPECAMI) Centre of Professional Courses Centre for Distance and Online
Education  Schools including one for the visually challenged.

The details of courses of studies and the eligibility requirement for admission to each course have

been outlined in this Guide. Admissions in all the courses are done strictly as per merit on the basis

of rules framed by the Academic Council for each course of study as amended and enforced from
time to time. Further, admissions to AMU, Aligarh as well as AMU Centre at Malappuram,

Murshidabad and Kishaanganj will be made through a single admission process for courses of study

being taught at more than one location.

RESIDENTIAL LIFE

Students are normally allocated a Hall of Residence at the time of admission. A Hall of Residence

is a cluster of hostels administered by a Provost. Facilities such as Reading Room, Common Room,

indoor and outdoor games are available in almost all Halls of Residence.

In view of the limited residential facility for students there is no guarantee of hostel

accommodation. Accommodation to students allocated a Hall of Residence will be provided as per

the policy / rules laid down by the University, subject to the availability of seats in the hostel. Unless

specified otherwise, candidates admitted to Evening / Part Time courses and courses running under

Centre of Professional Courses and Centre for Distance & Online Education shall not be provided
hostel accommodation.

Local students or those students who are not desirous of residential accommodation are designated

as non-resident students. Non-Resident male students are allotted Non-Resident Students Centre

(NRSC) while the female students are attached with one of the Hall of Residence for women
students.

DISCIPLINE

The University Proctor and his associates are responsible for maintaining discipline and security in
the campus. Deans of Faculties, Principals of Schools / Colleges / Polytechnics and Chairmen of

Departments of Studies ensure orderly behaviour of the students in the Faculties, Colleges /

Polytechnics / Schools and Departments respectively, while Provosts and Wardens do the same in

the Halls of Residence.

RAGGING

Ragging is banned in the University campus and is a punishable offence as per AMU Student’s
Conduct and Discipline Rule, 1985.

The student and his/her parent/guardian will have to submit an “Undertaking” on prescribed format

to the effect that the student shall not take part in any form of ragging and shall also abide by the

rules prescribed for the purpose as amended and enforced from time to time.


3

IMPORTANT INFORMATION AND RULES

```
Important information and Rules pertaining to admission for the session 2026 - 27 are as given
below and are part of the Guide to Admissions which can be seen / downloaded from the
Controller’s Office website:
```
[http://www.amucontrollerexams.com](http://www.amucontrollerexams.com)

```
The candidate who applies for admission is advised to carefully read the same and it shall be
presumed that he/she agrees to abide by the same.
```
1. Admissions to all courses of study as detailed in this Guide are open to Indian Nationals
    only. A few seats are also earmarked for foreign nationals/children of Non-resident Indians
    (NRI). Candidates applying under foreign national/children of Non-resident Indians category
    should refer to the relevant Guide/Supplement for them.
2. The intake to all courses of study as detailed in this Guide, except those specifically
    mentioned for AMU Centres at Malappuram, Murshidabad and/or Kishanganj, implies intake
    at Aligarh Muslim University, Aligarh only.
3. The intake to all courses of study as detailed in this Guide is only indicative of the maximum
    intake capacity of each course of study and does not bind the University to admit the number
    of students specified.
4. The University may change/modify the notified Intake, eligibility criteria, admission processes
    anytime without giving any prior notification. Changes, if any, in this regard shall be updated
    on the University website and will be applicable to candidates seeking admission in the
    University even after notification.
5. The University reserves the right not to admit any candidate to a course of study even though
    a notification inviting applications for admission to the same has been issued.
6. In some of the courses of studies there is provision for supernumerary “PAID / SELF
    FINANCE SEATS”. The details of all such Courses of Studies, number of seats earmarked
    and the additional chargeable fee on per annum basis have been notified separately. The
    desirous candidates are advised to keep track of all such notices.
7. If number of applicants for a particular course of study is less than the notified intake, the
    University reserves the right not to run such a course of study.
8. A candidate shall be eligible to apply for admission to a course of study if he/she has passed
    the qualifying examination and also fulfills all other eligibility requirements in terms of subjects
    studied, percentage of marks, age, etc. The percentage of marks secured by a candidate at
    the qualifying examination, falling short by even a decimal fraction shall not be rounded off to
    the next whole number. Similarly, if the age falls short or exceeds even by a single day, the
    candidate shall not be eligible for admission.
9. Candidates awaiting result of qualifying examination may also apply for admission with the
    clear stipulation that in the event of their selection they will be entitled to admission only if
    they fulfill all eligibility requirements of concerned course of study at the time of counselling /
    admission.
10. Unless specified otherwise, for admission to a M.A./M.Sc./M.Com. courses in various
    Faculties where the qualifying examination is B.A./B.Sc./B.Com. degree, the candidates must
    ensure that they fulfill the eligibility requirement in terms of qualifying examination in respect
    of the Major / Minor Subject defined as follows:
       a) Major Subject: It is the subject studied by the candidate as the primary discipline of
          study, forming the main focus of Bachelor’s degree (approx. 50% of credits)
       b) Minor Subject: Besides Major Subject, other subject (excluding Vocational Subjects,
          Value added Subjects, Skill based Subjects, Generic Subjects) studied by the
          candidate at Bachelor’s degree Level (approx. 20% of credits).
11. B.A. /B.Sc. /B.Com. degrees prescribed as the eligibility requirement for various Course of
    Studies in this Guide are four-year Degree Courses under the 10+2+ 4 system of education.


4

12. Eligibility rules as specified for each course shall be strictly followed and shall not be relaxed
    under any circumstance. Before applying, the candidate should satisfy himself/herself that
    he/she fulfills the eligibility requirements prescribed for admission to the concerned course of
    study.
13. The candidates should also refer to Table-II detailing ‘Allowed Courses’ to ascertain the
    courses for which they are permitted to apply as per their qualification, age and eligibility.
14. While applying for various courses of study, the candidate is advised to consult the schedule
    of Admission/Departmental Test, wherever applicable, so as to ensure that there is no clash
    in the Test schedule of various courses for which the candidate is applying for admission.
    The University assumes no responsibility if the candidate has opted for more than one course
    of study for which the Tests have been scheduled simultaneously.
15. Eligibility Criteria as a consolidation of two or more Mark-sheets/Grade-Sheets of
    different Issuing Authorities will not be considered.
16. No candidate will be eligible to take admission to the same Course / Class to which he/she
    was admitted earlier.
17. Use of unfair means/impersonation in Admission/Departmental Test and canvassing in any
    manner for securing admission shall render a candidate disqualified. Further, the University
    will be free to take any legal action against him/her as per law.
18. A candidate whose qualifying examination is not recognized by this University shall not be
    eligible for admission. All such Application Forms / admissions shall be rejected / cancelled.
19. Definition of Internal/External: An Internal candidate is one who has passed the qualifying
    examination conducted by THIS University as a regular student not earlier than THREE (3)
    academic years from the date of admission to the Course he/she is seeking admission to.
    And all other candidates shall be treated as External.
    Internal candidates are required to upload relevant documents with their Application Form in
    support of internal status, failing which they may be considered as External candidates.
    Note: Students permitted to appear in various examinations of the University as Private /
    Distance mode candidates, shall not be entitled for consideration under the Internal category.
20. Unless specified otherwise, candidates are required to fill separate Application Forms (only
    in the Online Mode) for each course of study as detailed in this Guide. No relaxation in the
    last date for applying shall be permissible.
21. Application Forms shall not be transferred from one course of study to another under any
    circumstance.
22. For all courses where Selection Process is based on (or has a component of) candidate’s
    performance in the Qualifying Examination, the candidate must upload/submit self-attested
    copy of his/her marksheet / grade sheet of Qualifying Examination (both sides) on or before
    the 22.06.202 6 failing which his/her Application Form will be summarily REJECTED.
23. Applications once submitted cannot be withdrawn. Candidates must note that mere deduction
    of Test fee/Processing charges from the bank account is not proof of fee payment. The
    payment should also be reflected on candidate’s application dashboard failing which it will
    not be considered as successful submission of application.
24. Incomplete applications and applications not in accordance with instructions are liable to be
    rejected without any further intimation.
25. The Test fee/Processing charges once deposited will not be refunded. The same will also not
    be carried forward to a future examination.
26. Admit Card to appear in the Admission / Departmental Test will be issued by the University
    only to those candidates whose Application form, complete in all respects, has been
    submitted successfully on the Controller’s website on or before the last date of filling as
    notified in this Guide.
    The University may neither verify the information filled by the candidates in the application
    form nor verify any uploaded certificate of category/educational qualification for deciding the
    eligibility of candidates before the Test. The certificates of educational qualification and
    special category will be examined at the time of counselling / physical reporting. The
    University will, in no way, be responsible for any wrong/incorrect information furnished by the
    candidate(s) in their online application form.


5

27. No Admit Card shall be sent by post. For Admission/Departmental Test Courses, Admit
    Cards will only be downloadable from the Controller’s website
       [http://www.amucontrollerexams.com](http://www.amucontrollerexams.com)
28. The candidate is required to paste his/her recent passport size colour photograph in the
    space provided on the downloaded Admit Card (same as affixed on the Application Form).
    The candidate will not be allowed to enter the Test Centre if he/she is not in possession
    of proper Admit Card with duly affixed photograph of the candidate.
29. The candidate should contact immediately the concerned Application Form handling Office
    in case of any discrepancy in the Admit Card in order to avoid any last-minute
    inconvenience. University assumes no responsibility whatsoever in the event of failure to
    report on the due date and time by the candidate for appearing in the Admission /
    Departmental Test.
30. The medium of all Tests shall be English, except where a question paper is set in a language
    other than English. The Test paper syllabi are given on the Controller’s website.
31. The University reserves the right to make changes in the notified Admission Test /
    Departmental Test/Counselling Schedule.
32. In case a candidate who does not fulfil the conditions of eligibility prescribed for the concerned
    course of study, appears in the Admission / Departmental Test, he/she shall be doing so at
    his/her own risk and cost, and if at any stage, it is found that the candidate does not fulfil the
    eligibility requirements, the admission, if granted, shall be cancelled ipso facto.
33. Scribe will be provided to the visually challenged candidates appearing in Admission /
    Departmental Test. However, such candidates must submit a written request for the same at
    the time of applying. Blind candidates who have been provided with a Scribe may be given
    an additional time to the extent of 33 % of the Test duration.
34. No candidate securing less than 20% marks in the Admission Test/ Departmental Test,
    wherever applicable, shall be eligible for admission in the concerned course of study.
35. No separate intimation letters will be sent to the candidates short-listed for interview /
    Group Discussion/Counselling (wherever applicable) or selected for admission. The
    lists of candidates shortlisted for Interview/G.D./Counselling and the lists of those selected
    for admission will be displayed on the Controller’s website. The dates notified for Interview /
    G.D. / counselling/admission shall strictly be followed. It is the responsibility of the candidates
    to keep themselves informed from the website or through their own sources whether their
    names appear in the displayed lists and thereby make timely arrangements to appear for
    Interview/G.D./ counselling/ admission or for physical reporting, as the case may be. The
    University shall not be responsible if a candidate fails to get information regarding his/her
    shortlisting for Interview/G.D./Counselling or selection for admission.
36. The absence of a candidate in any component of the Admission / Departmental Test including
    Written Test, Group Discussion, Interview etc., as the case may be, shall forfeit his/her claim
    for admission in the said course of study.
37. The University may issue or display `Chance Memo List’ in addition to the list of selected
    candidates. Chance Memo is not an offer of admission but is issued only in case there is
    likelihood of a vacancy due to any reason. Chance Memo list, if any, shall be displayed on
    the Controller’s website. It is the responsibility of the candidate to keep track of all such
    notices. No separate intimation letters will be sent to the candidates offered Chance
    Memos.
38. Counselling schedule for each course of study, wherever applicable, shall be notified by the
    University in due course of time.
39. Candidates shortlisted for counselling (on Select/Chance Memo List) shall report for
    counselling and clearly specify their order of preference of Course / Branch / Major Subject /
    Stream / Specialization/School from among those listed under the concerned course of study
    as per notified schedule and procedure.
    Failure on the part of a short-listed candidate to report for counselling or not completing the
    steps as notified in the counselling procedure shall forfeit his/her claim for admission. The
    offer of counselling/admission shall stand cancelled and no correspondence in this regard
    shall be entertained.


6

40. Selected candidates shall be allotted Course/ Branch/ Major Subject/ Stream/
    Specialization/School on merit, as per preference indicated by them. A candidate who has
    been selected for a higher preference will have no claim for lower preferences.
41. A candidate provisionally admitted to a Course / Branch / Major Subject / Stream /
    Specialization / School shall be upgraded automatically, on merit, to another Course/ Branch/
    Major Subject/ Stream/ Specialization/School of higher preference in the event of a vacancy
    arising therein.
    However, a candidate admitted/upgraded to a Course/ Branch/ Main Subject/ Stream/
    Specialization/School shall be permitted to retain the same if he/she submits an undertaking
    on the Counselling portal on the date of his/her admission / upgradation for not upgrading it
    any further.
42. The candidate admitted/upgraded to a particular course of study either at AMU, Aligarh or
    any of the AMU Centres at Malappuram, Murshidabad & Kishanganj shall not be allowed to
    change the Study Centre after the notified closing date of admissions.
43. Any seat that remains unfilled after the completion of admissions of candidates on the Select
    list shall be filled up by the candidate who had reported with reference to his/her Chance
    Memo as per notified scheduled for reporting, if any, strictly in order of Chance Memo
    Number. However, if such a vacancy arises after the closing date of admissions, the vacancy
    shall not be filled up and the same shall remain unfilled.
44. Candidates will have to upload image of original Mark sheet of the qualifying examination,
    with the requisite percentage of marks, and all other relevant Certificates/Documents at the
    time of Counselling.
45. The candidate who possess the Internet downloaded marks-sheet / grade-sheet of qualifying
    examination may be considered for provisional admission to the course concerned if the
    same is attested by the Controller / Registrar / Issuing Authority of the concerned University
    / Board or Principal / Head of the School / College / Institution concerned.
46. If the result of qualifying examination of a candidate has not been declared at the time of
    counselling, such a candidate will not be eligible for provisional admission. Candidates
    awaiting results of their Annual / Supplementary / Compartmental / Improvement examination
    shall not be considered for admission.
47. No candidate shall be admitted unless he/she has completed all the eligibility requirements
    at the time of admission. Candidates enjoying employed status and selected for admission
    to any full-time course of study in the University, are required to produce leave sanction
    and/or relieving order at the time of counselling from their employer for the duration of the
    course permitting them to pursue their studies at the University, failing which the offer of
    admission shall stand withdrawn.
48. All offer of admissions shall be provisional and shall be subject to clearance from the Office
    of the Proctor.
49. No candidate shall be entitled to claim admission as a matter of right.
50. All provisionally admitted candidates shall have to mandatorily report in person and produce
    the original Mark-sheet of the qualifying examination at the time of physical reporting /
    verification as per notified schedule and no extension shall be given in this regard on any
    ground whatsoever.
    Any other document (sealed and/or confidential statement of marks), other than a proper
    mark-sheet, even if issued by the Controller / Registrar / Head of the Institution etc. of the
    concerned University / Board / Institution in regard to marks / grades obtained by a candidate
    shall not be entertained at the time of physical reporting by the candidate under any
    circumstances.
    If any discrepancy is found in the examination result of the aforesaid candidate or the original
    Marksheet/Grade sheet is not submitted by the candidate within stipulated time, the
    University reserves the right to cancel the provisional admission of such a candidate with no
    refund of admission charges / fee.
51. The candidate selected for admission shall have to submit the Original Migration and
    Character Certificate from the Head of the Institution/University last attended at the time of
    physical reporting. Candidate who is not in a position to submit the Migration and/or Character


7

```
Certificate at the time of physical reporting, shall give an undertaking on prescribed Proforma
(as given in Appendix) to submit the same on or before 30.09.202 6 , failing which the
University reserves the right to cancel his/her admission with no refund of admission charges
/ fee.
```
52. Admitted candidates who have qualified GATE/JRF or any other Scholarship provided by a
    national funding agency will be given the same subject to the condition that they fulfil the
    eligibility requirements of the concerned scholarship and the grant for disbursing the
    scholarship is provided to the University by AICTE/UGC/funding agency/DBT payment.
53. If any error / omission in the processing / verification of Application Form / certificates /
    documents / eligibility of a candidate is detected after the candidate is admitted to a course
    in the University, the University has the right to cancel such admission at any stage at which
    the error/ omission is detected with no refund of admission charges / fee.
54. If it is found, at any stage, that a candidate
    a) does not fulfil the eligibility requirements
    b) has used fraudulent means to secure admission
    c) has made false or incorrect statement(s) in the Application Form
    d) has not uploaded his/her signature/photo/thumb impression on the Application Form
       or has uploaded the same of somebody else.
    then he/she shall not be allowed to complete the admission formalities, or in case already
    admitted, his/her admission shall be cancelled, ipso facto.
55. If at any stage, the original documents relating to a candidate’s admission are found to be
    fake/non-genuine or fabricated or in any other manner defective, the concerned candidate
    will not be admitted and if already admitted, admission will be cancelled without any prior
    notice in this regard. No fee shall be refunded in such cases. The University reserves the
    right to take appropriate legal action against such a candidate. If the forgery is detected after
    completion of the course by the candidate, the University reserves the right to cancel his/her
    Degree/Diploma/Certificate.
56. In case of cancellation of admission by a candidate, the admission charges/fee of any kind
    paid by him/her will be refunded as per rules for Refund of Fee.
57. The University reserves the right to deny admission to any candidate/applicant seeking
    admission to any course of study who has been found indulging in any criminal, illegal or anti-
    social activities and whose presence in the University campus will be detrimental to peaceful
    atmosphere in the University. A candidate who is suspended, rusticated, debarred, expelled
    etc. by the University shall not be eligible for claiming admission in any course of study
    whatsoever.
58. The University reserves the right to get any student medically examined and if found
    medically unfit, the admission of such student will be cancelled.
59. A student, other than a Ph.D. scholar, can pursue simultaneously:
    - two full time academic programmes in physical mode, both from this University or one
       from this University and another from any other University, only if the class timings for
       one programme do not overlap with the class timings of the other programme.
    - two academic programmes, one in Full-time Physical mode/ Open and Distance
       Learning (ODL) mode/Online mode from this University and another in Open and
       Distance Learning (ODL) mode/Online mode; from this or any other University.
60. Admitted candidates are required to declare the details of all courses of studies being pursued
    simultaneously by them on prescribed Proforma. In case of any concealment / mis-
    representation, the University reserves the right to cancel the provisional admission of such
    a candidate with no refund of admission charges / fee.
61. No candidate admitted to a full-time course of study in the University shall accept or hold any
    employment paid or otherwise or get involved in any business or commercial relation with the
    University during the course of his/her study at the University except those specifically
    permitted by the University in accordance with rules.
62. The Following procedure shall be applicable for admission to the Courses of Studies based
    on CUET(UG) Score:


8

- Register and submit the form for the concerned Course of Study at Aligarh Muslim
    University on the website: cuet.samarth.ac.in
- Must take the CUET(UG)- 2026 Entrance Test in the specified Domain/ General/
    Languages Sections of CUET for the concerned Course of Study
- Fill Online Application Form of Aligarh Muslim University on the website:
    [http://www.amucontrollerexams.com](http://www.amucontrollerexams.com) for the concerned Course of Study specifying CUET
    Application number in AMU Application Form.
- Register and participate in Counselling, if shortlisted for admission.
63. Application No./ Roll No. should be quoted for all queries or correspondence and at the time
of submission of required documents. The documents submitted without mentioning
Application No./ Roll No. will not be considered.
64. No correspondence shall be made to candidates not selected for admission and the
documents / certificates uploaded by such candidates shall not be returned.
65. In case of any ambiguity in the interpretation of any of the instructions/ terms/ rules/
regulations/ criteria/processes regarding the determination of information contained in this
Guide to Admissions, eligibility, registration of candidates, allocation of Test Centre, issuance
of Admit Card, the conduct of Test, publication of Result, counselling and admission, the
interpretation /determination of the University shall be final and binding on all candidates.
66. Information uploaded on the website shall not be provided to the candidate or any other
person under R.T.I. Act, 2005. Further, the information uploaded on the website shall remain
there for a limited period only. Therefore, the candidates are advised to download the
uploaded information and keep it with them for the future. In due course of the Test or the
midway of admission process, neither any application under the Right to Information Act,
2005 shall be entertained nor information will be provided.
67. The Answer Sheets and other relevant material pertaining to the Admission / Departmental
Test(s) of all the candidates and Application Forms of all the non-admitted candidates will be
weeded out after 04 months of declaration of result of Admission / Departmental Test
concerned. Therefore, in case of any dispute regarding admission, the matter must be filed
within 04 months declaration of result of Admission / Departmental Test concerned after
which the relevant records may not be made available.
68. Any dispute with regard to any matter relating to admission in the University and its Centres
shall be subject to the jurisdiction of High Court of Judicature at Allahabad, Uttar Pradesh
only.
69. The closing date for all admissions in the University, except those courses / categories for
which separate notification will be made, is 31.08.202 6. Any vacancy arising after this date
in any course shall not be filled.
70. All provisionally admitted students will have to fill “Student Registration Form” giving full
details about themselves on the designated portal as per schedule notified by the University.
The students will also be required to choose the list of Compulsory and Elective papers they
intend to study in the ensuing semester/year after participating in the registration counselling,
wherever applicable.

RULES FOR ADMISSION OF PERSONS WITH BENCHMARK DISABILITIES

1. 5% seats are reserved for Persons with Benchmark Disabilities (PwBD) in various courses
    of study over and above the approved intake, wherever applicable. However, for MBBS, BDS,
    BUMS, B.Sc. Nursing, B.Arch., P.G. courses in the Faculty of Medicine/Unani Medicine and
    Ph.D. courses, the reservation will be within the approved intake only.
2. Only those eligible candidates shall be considered for admission under the PwBD category
    who have degree of disability to a minimum extent of 40% as prescribed in the “THE RIGHTS
    OF PERSONS WITH DISABILITIES ACT, 2016”.
3. Such candidates would be considered for admission only to those courses of study/disciplines
    where their physical disability is not considered as a hindrance in pursuing the course of
    study.


9

4. PwBD candidates have to pay only Rs.100.00 as Admission Test Fee/Pocessing Charges at
    the time of applying.
5. PwBD candidates, if selected, will have to pay only Rs.100.00 towards Admission Charges
    (Tuition Fee) at the time of admission. However, such exemption will not be valid for those
    PwBD students who have been awarded Fellowship or if admitted against seats earmarked
    under Self Finance, NRI or Foreign national category.
6. Candidates under this category shall be given relaxation to the extent of 5% marks in the
    qualifying examination and shall also be given relaxation to the extent of 5% marks in the
    Admission/Departmental Test to determine their eligibility for admission in the University.
7. Candidates under this category shall be given a relaxation in age up to a maximum of five
    years in admission to courses which prescribe a maximum age limit, except for those courses
    where such limits are prescribed by Statutory/Regulatory Councils governing such
    admissions.
8. In case eligible candidates under the PwBD category are not available for admission to
    courses where the reservation is within the approved Annual intake, the unfilled seats shall
    be transferred to General Category (not applicable for Ph.D. programme).
9. The Disability Certificate of the candidate should be issued by the Medical Board of the
    District/State/UT/Medical Institution of National Importance.
10. All provisionally admitted candidates who had claimed PwBD category at the time of applying
    will be examined by a duly constituted Medical Board of the University to determine the
    degree / extent of disability of the concerned candidates, whose decision in the matter shall
    be final.
11. Candidates must note that the benefit of reservation will be given to them subject to
    verification of documents. If it is discovered at any stage that a candidate has used a
    false/fake/incorrect document, or has furnished false, incorrect, or incomplete information, in
    order to avail the benefit of reservation, then such a candidate shall be excluded from all
    admission processes. In case such a candidate has already been given admission, the
    admission shall stand cancelled.
12. The qualified candidates seeking admission under PwBD Category in MBBS / BDS courses
    of the University will get themselves certified ONLY at one of the designated centres as
    specified in the NEET(UG)- 2026 bulletin before reporting.

```
RULES FOR ADMISSION AGAINST SEATS EARMARKED FOR ADMISSION UNDER
CO-CURRICULAR / EXTRA-CURRICULAR ACTIVITIES
```
A. OUTSTANDING SPORTSPERSON CATEGORY

1. Candidate must choose the outstanding sportsperson category and upload certificates of
    achievements in the relevant game/sports while filling the Application Form for the course
    concerned and also pay an additional Processing charge of Rs.150.00, failing which he/she
    will forfeit his/her claim for consideration under this category. Sports certificates will not be
    accepted after submission of Application Form.
2. Candidate can choose only one game/sports in which he/she wishes to be considered for
    participating in the Sports trial in a given Academic Session while filling the Application Form
    for various course of studies.
3. The uploaded Sports Certificates should be not more than two years old. For the session
    2026 - 27 , the certificates issued for the events organized from 01.01. 2024 only will be
    considered.
4. Sports certificates issued by Federations/Associations approved by Indian Olympic
    Association (IOA)/ Khelo India/ Association of Indian Universities OR certificate issued by
    University for participation in Zonal or All India Inter University competitions shall only be
    considered.
    In case there is more than one Association / Federation in any game, the sports certificates
    issued by those concerned game Associations/Federations will be considered which are
    recognized by National Federation of the concerned game duly recognized by Ministry of
    Sports and Youth Affairs, India and duly registered under the concerned Indian Act.


10

5. The Invitational / Memorial / Open / Prize Money / Ranking tournament Certificates will not
    be considered
6. Certificates on Letter head will not be considered.
7. Admission will be offered only in Sports / Specialization in which Association of Indian
    Universities organizes Intervarsity and Clubs for such Sports / Specialization exist in the
    University. (viz. Athletics, Cricket, Football, Badminton, Basketball, Volleyball, Table Tennis,
    Wrestling, Weightlifting, Powerlifting, Skating, Hockey, Swimming, Tennis).
    Along with the above-mentioned games:
       - Horse-Riding will also be considered as eligible sports discipline for admission under
          Outstanding Sportsperson Category provided the candidate has equivalent
          achievements in EFI organized/approved events (Dressage, Show Jumping, Tent
          Pegging).
       - Hiking & Mountaineering will also be considered as eligible sports discipline for
          admission under Outstanding Sportsperson Category provided the candidate has
          completed Mountaineering Course / Rock-Climbing Course / Snow Skiing Course
          (Basic course for UG admissions and Advanced course for PG admissions) from a
          recognized mountaineering institute.
8. For admission to Post Graduate Courses, representing the University at least once in the
    Zonal/All-India Inter-varsity (wherever applicable) shall be mandatory.
9. Application Form for admission under Outstanding Sportsperson category shall be applicable
    only for those courses where seats have been earmarked for the same (over and above the
    approved intake for the concerned course of study) as given in Table IV.
10. Filling up of Outstanding Sportsperson Proforma along with the Application Form does not
    guarantee that the candidate will be called for trial by the University.
11. Appearance in the Admission/Departmental Test of the course concerned and securing at
    least minimum marks prescribed to be eligible for admission under General Category will be
    the mandatory requirement for short-listing for Sports trial / admission.
12. Applicants short-listed for trial will have to appear in Physical Fitness Test followed by Sports
    Skill Trial at Aligarh as per schedule notified by the University.
    Physical Fitness Test (PFT): PFT will only be a qualifier. The components of PFT
    (separately for Male & Female candidates) will be notified by the University Games
    Committee.
    Sports Skill Trials: Only PFT qualified candidates would be eligible for sports skill trials. The
    Sports Skill Trial will comprise of:
       - Fundamental Skills in the concerned game.
       - Game Performance in Trials.
13. The list of the candidates called for trial will be uploaded on the University website
    [http://www.amucontrollerexams.com](http://www.amucontrollerexams.com) one-two weeks before the trials. No intimation will be sent
    by post/email. Candidates are advised to check / visit the University website regularly for
    updates.
14. Candidates shortlisted for trials shall travel to Aligarh and stay for the entire duration of the
    Trials under their own arrangement. No TA/DA shall be admissible.
15. Candidates not reporting for the trial on due date and time shall forfeit their claim for
    admission under Outstanding Sportsperson category.
16. Candidates short-listed for trial shall be required to produce a valid proof of Identity
    (Aadhar/Passport/PAN-Card/Driving License/Identity Card of the Institution last
    attended/Voter-ID etc.) at the time of reporting along with a self-certified copy of the same.
17. Candidates seeking admission under Outstanding Sportsperson category shall have to
    submit their respective playing position on the field for team event at the time of reporting for
    trial/filling of Application Form.
18. Candidates shall have to submit Undertaking for Physical Fitness Test at the time of reporting
    for trial before the Physical Fitness Test. The University takes no responsibility for any injury
    incurred to the candidate during the Trial.
19. Candidates are required to produce original Certificates of achievements and mark-sheet of
    the qualifying examination at the time of trial / admission.


11

20. Candidates shall also submit an Undertaking at the time of reporting for trial that they will
    attend the grounds regularly and will have 75% attendance at the sports ground and would
    also participate in the Inter-Hall, Inter-College, Inter-Faculty, Inter-University, State, National
    and International sports tournaments if admitted to the University under Outstanding
    Sportsperson Category. Their admission would be liable to be cancelled or alternatively they
    will not be allowed to sit in the University examinations if the terms of the undertaking thus
    given are not adhered to.
21. Participation in Sports trials by a candidate does not guarantee the offer of admission. The
    trial is only to check the claim made by the candidate that he/she is an Outstanding
    Sportsperson.
22. Only those candidates who fulfil the Academic and Sports eligibility as given in Guide to
    Admission and Association of Indian Universities (AIU) participation rules, wherever
    applicable, will be considered for admission irrespective of invitation to appear for sports trial.
    However, relaxation in the academic eligibility (aggregate percentage) up to 5% in aggregate
    percentage (as applicable under General category), if required, will be given for admission
    under Outstanding Sportsperson category.
23. The decision of the University in all matters relating to eligibility, acceptance or rejection of
    Application and selection of candidates shall be final and binding on the candidates and no
    enquiry or correspondence shall be entertained in this regard.
24. Unless specified otherwise, only a maximum of one seat per Course of Study / Major Subject
    / Branch / Specialization etc. will be allocated to candidates under Outstanding Sportsperson
    category during counselling.
25. Immediately after admissions, the Original Sports Certificates will be submitted by the
    admitted candidates in the University Games Committee to get them verified. The certificates
    shall be returned to the candidates only after verification/one academic year.
26. The University shall have the authority to cancel admission at any time, if it is found that the
    candidate has obtained such admission on the basis of a false/forged certificate and such a
    candidate shall be liable to face legal proceedings / criminal prosecution.
27. The Closing Date for admissions under Outstanding Sportsperson category will be
    31.08.202 6. Any vacancy arising after this date in any course of study shall not be filled.

(^)
SPORTS ELIGIBILITY FOR ADMISSION UNDER OUTSTANDING SPORTSPERSON
CATEGORY
Senior Secondary School / Diploma in Engineering:
Participation in CBSE / ICSE / KVS / JNV / EMRS / State Board Schools, Zonal / Clusters /
National Sports Meet. (For Internal Students, participation in the School Team in Inter-School
competition organized by the Directorate of School Education, AMU)
OR
Representation of the State in the annual regular competition of National Championships of
various games of different age groups, organize by the recognized Federation / Association /
Organisation / Board approved by the Indian Olympic Association (IOA) / Mnistry of Sports and
Youth Affairs (MSYA), and duly registered under the concerned Indian Act.
OR
Representation of the country at the international level in any age group. Such competitions
should have been approved by the Indian Olympic Association (IOA), Sports Authority of India
(SAI) or the Ministry of Youth Affairs and Sports (MYAS)
Undergraduate Programmes:
Secured any of the first three positions in CBSE/KVS/JNV, School Nationals and Sports Boards
tournaments under SGFI or have represented the All India Combined Schools Teams.
OR
Represented the state in the National Championship, of various age groups, organized by the
recognized Federations of India.
OR
Represented India at the International level in any age group.

B. INVITED CATEGORY FOR OUTSTANDING SPORTSPERSON:

1. Outstanding Sportspersons having significantly higher achievements in sports and have
    represented: India at the International level / State or Combined Universities team at the
    National level / University concerned at the All-India level at least once or University
    concerned at the Zonal level twice in the last two years may be considered for admission
    under ‘Invited Category’.
2. Candidates to be admitted under ‘Invited Category’ will neither be required to appear in the
    Admission Test of the course concerned nor appear for the Sports trial but should fulfil all
    other academic and sports eligibility requirements as applicable for candidates being
    admitted through trials.
3. Admission under ‘Invited Category’ will be offered in all courses of studies at Under Graduate
    and Post-Graduate level (except Ph.D.), over and above the approved intake for the
    concerned course of study, except for courses being offered in the Faculties of Medicine,
    Unani Medicine and Engineering & Technology subject to fulfilling the eligibility requirements
    of the University and AIU participation rules.

C. OUTSTANDING DEBATER & TALENT CATEGORY

1. Candidate must choose the Outstanding Debater & Talent Category and upload certificates
    of achievements in the relevant sub-category while filling the Application Form for the course
    concerned, failing which he/she will forfeit his/her claim for consideration under this category.
    Certificates will not be accepted after submission of Application Form.
2. Candidate can choose only one sub-category (Debater / Creative & Journalistic Writing /
    Dramatics / Music / Fine Arts) in which he/she wishes to be considered for participating in the
    trial in a given Academic Session while filling the Application Form for various course of
    studies.
3. The uploaded Sports Certificates should be not more than two years old. For the session
    2026 - 27 , the certificates issued for the events organized from 01.01.202 4 only will be
    considered.
4. Achievement certificates issued by Association of Indian University OR certificate issued by
    University for participation in Zonal or All India Inter University competitions or by
    CBSE/KVS/JNV etc organized All-India/Zonal/State events duly recognized by Ministry of
    Sports and Youth Affairs/Culture, India shall only be considered.
5. The Invitational / Memorial / Open / Prize Money / Ranking tournament Certificates will not
    be considered.
6. Certificates on Letter head will not be considered.
7. For admission to PG Courses, representing the University at least once in the Zonal/All-India
    Inter-varsity (wherever applicable) shall be mandatory.
8. Application Form for admission under Outstanding Debater & Talent category shall be
    applicable only for those courses where seats have been earmarked for the same (over and
    above the approved intake for the concerned course of study) as given in Table V.
9. Filling up of Outstanding Debater & Talent category Proforma along with the Application Form
    does not guarantee that the candidate will be called for trial by the University.
10. Appearance in the Admission/Departmental Test of the course concerned and securing at
    least minimum marks prescribed to be eligible for admission under General Category will be
    the mandatory requirement for short-listing for trial / admission.


13

11. Applicants short-listed for trial will have to appear in Debater & Talent Skill Test at Aligarh as
    per schedule notified by the University.
12. The list of the candidates called for trial will be uploaded on the University website
    [http://www.amucontrollerexams.com](http://www.amucontrollerexams.com) one-two weeks before the trials. No intimation will be sent by
    post/email. Candidates are advised to check / visit the University website regularly for
    updates.
13. Candidates shortlisted for trials shall travel to Aligarh and stay for the entire duration of the
    Trials under their own arrangement. No TA/DA shall be admissible.
14. Candidates not reporting for the trial on due date and time shall forfeit their claim for
    admission under Outstanding Debater & Talent category.
15. Candidates short-listed for trial shall be required to produce a valid proof of Identity
    (Aadhar/Passport/PAN-Card/Driving License/Identity Card of the Institution last
    attended/Voter I-Card) at the time of reporting along with a self-certified copy of the same.
16. Candidates are required to produce original Certificates of achievements and mark-sheet of
    the qualifying examination at the time of trial / admission.
17. Candidates shall also submit an Undertaking at the time of reporting for trial that they will
    attend the Cultural Education Centre (CEC) activities regularly and must have 75%
    attendance at the CEC / University notified Centre / Club and would also participate in the
    Inter-Hall, Inter-College, Inter-Faculty, Inter-University, State, National and International
    tournaments if admitted to the University under Outstanding Debater & Talent Category. Their
    admission would be liable to be cancelled or alternatively they will not be allowed to sit in the
    University examinations if the terms of the undertaking thus given are not adhered to.
18. Participation in Debater & Talent trials by a candidate does not guarantee the offer of
    admission. The trial is only to check the claim made by the candidate.
19. Only those candidates who fulfil the Academic and Debater & Talent category eligibility as
    given in Guide to Admission and Association of Indian Universities (AIU) participation rules,
    wherever applicable, will be considered for admission irrespective of invitation to appear for
    trial. However, relaxation in the academic eligibility (aggregate percentage) up to 5% in
    aggregate percentage (as applicable under General category), if required, will be given for
    admission under Outstanding Debater & Talent category.
20. The decision of the University in all matters relating to eligibility, acceptance or rejection of
    Application and selection of candidates shall be final and binding on the candidates and no
    enquiry or correspondence shall be entertained in this regard.
21. Unless specified otherwise, only a maximum of one seat per Course of Study / Major Subject
    / Branch / Specialization etc. will be allocated to candidates under Outstanding Debater &
    Talent category during counselling.
22. Immediately after admissions, the Original Debater & Talent Certificates will be submitted by
    the admitted candidates in the Cultural Education Centre to get them verified through the
    Controller’s Office. The certificates shall be returned to the candidates only after
    verification/one academic year.
23. The University shall have the authority to cancel admission at any time, if it is found that the
    candidate has obtained such admission on the basis of a false/forged certificate and such a
    candidate shall be liable to face legal proceedings / criminal prosecution.
24. The Closing Date for admissions under Outstanding Debater & Talent category will be
    31.08.202 6. Any vacancy arising after this date in any course of study shall not be filled.

PROCEDURE FOR DEBATER & TALENT CATEGORY TRIALS:

Debate: English, Hindi & Urdu

1. The motion for the debate as well as the side (for or against the motion) will be given to
    the candidates on the spot at the venue. The candidates will not have the freedom to
    choose the side of the motion.
2. Each candidate will be given a maximum of four (3 + 1) minutes to speak. He/she will get
    05 minutes preparation time.
3. Candidates will be evaluated overall on the basis of their content, logical argumentation,
    manner of presentation. Emotional, obstinate and ornamental speech lacking content and
    logic will be penalised.
4. Candidates are advised to bring pen and paper to help them prepare their arguments.
    However, reading out from the paper while debating will not be allowed (the candidates
    can at most look at their jottings time to time).
5. Possession and use of mobile phone / any other electronic device is strictly prohibited

during the trial.^
Music: Indian / Western

1. Each candidate will be required to introduce the item/Raag & Taal in not more than 30
    seconds.
2. Each candidate will be given a maximum of 3 minutes to perform.
3. Musical instrument, if needed by the candidate, may be provided subject to availability.
4. Possession and use of mobile phone / any other electronic device is strictly prohibited

```
during the trial.^
Creative & Journalistic Writing: English, Hindi & Urdu
```
1. Topics will be announced at the venue.
2. Candidates will have to complete writing in a maximum of 500 words.
3. Candidates will be given 30 minutes to complete their work.
4. Possession and use of mobile phone / any other electronic device is strictly prohibited

during the trial.^

Fine Arts: Sketching & Painting

1. Candidates will be required to make still life drawing.
2. The candidate is expected to bring his/her own required drawing, sketching and painting
    material. No material shall be provided at the venue except an A3 water colour sheet.
3. Candidates will be given one hour to complete their work.
4. Candidates must bring their detailed portfolio at the time of trial.
5. Possession and use of mobile phone /any other electronic device is strictly prohibited
    during the trial.


15

Dramatics/Theatre:

1. Candidates will be required to create and perform a scene of 4-minutes duration on the
    basis of directions and elements provided on the spot.
2. Each candidate will be given a maximum of 5-minutes preparation time.
3. Candidates may be asked to discuss the scenes they have presented.
4. Candidates will be evaluated on the basis of scene content, innovative use of prescribed
    elements, acting ability and capacity for process analysis.
5. Candidates imitating film scenes, famous actors and using material from the internet will
    be penalised.
6. Candidates may present their scenes in Hindi, Urdu or English.
7. Possession and use of mobile phone / any other electronic device is strictly prohibited
    during the trial.

Maximum Age Limit for the purpose of admission

1. To safeguard the academic interest of students, the University is constrained to define the
    maximum age limit of the applicants for the purpose of admission to various course of studies
    as given under the concerned course of study.
2. Candidates shall be eligible to apply for admission to only those full-time regular courses of
    study where they have not exceeded the maximum age limit as permissible for that course.
3. Maximum Age Limit shall be reckoned on 01st July of the year of admission.
4. Maximum/Minimum Age Limit as prescribed by the regulatory bodies, wherever applicable,
    shall stand for that course of study.
5. Maximum Age Limit shall not be applicable for Foreign Nationals/ employees of the
    University.
6. Candidates who have passed the Qualifying Examination from Madarsa shall be given a
    relaxation upto three (03) years in the Maximum Age Limit for all course of studies.

ALLOWED COURSES:

(^)

1. To safeguard the academic interest of students, the University is constrained to define the
    following courses as allowed for the purpose of admission. Table-II gives the ‘Matrix for
    Allowed Courses’ wherein all full-time courses of study have been divided into four (04)
    Groups- A, B, C and D.
2. Courses within each Group have been further divided into various categories with Category
    1 being the lowest Category and Category 6 being the highest Category within a Group.
3. Candidates who have passed a course of study will be eligible to apply for admission to only
    those full-time regular courses of study as permissible by the following rules:
       (a) A person can do only one course of study from one category in a group.
       (b) Within a Group a person can move only from lower category to a higher category.
       (c) Persons from Group A can not go to any other group.
       (d) Persons from Group B can go to any category of Group A only.
       (e) Persons from Group C can go to any category of any other group.
       (f) Persons from Group D can go to any category of any other group.
4. Candidates can apply for B.Com.(Hons.) after passing Diploma in Secretarial Practice.
5. Candidates can apply for P.G. courses in the Faculty of Social Sciences after passing B.S.W.

Note: All the above rules regarding Allowed Courses are in addition to eligibility conditions, selection

procedures and such other conditions as applicable from time to time.

29

HOW TO OBTAIN AND FILL THE APPLICATION FORM

The entire application process for admission at Aligarh Muslim University is online, including

uploading of scanned images, Payment of Fees, and Printing of Confirmation Page. Therefore,

candidates are not required to send/submit any document(s) including Confirmation Page to the

University through Post/ Fax/By Hand.

- Candidates can apply for admission at Aligarh Muslim University only through Online mode.
    The Application Form, other than online mode, will not be accepted in any case.
- Only one application is to be submitted by a candidate for each course of study.
- Submission of Online Application Form may be done by accessing the University website
    [http://www.amucontrollerexams.com](http://www.amucontrollerexams.com) only.
- Candidates must follow the instructions strictly as given in the Guide to Admissions (202 6 -
    27 ) and on the website. Candidates not complying with the instructions shall be disqualified.
- Candidates must ensure that e-mail address and Mobile Number provided in the Online
    Application Form are their own or their parents’ as information/ communication, if any, to the
    candidate will be sent by the University through e-mail on e-mail address or SMS on given
    Mobile Number only. The University will not be responsible for non-receipt of latest
    information by the candidate due to wrong mobile number / e-mail ID filled in the Online
    Application Form.
- Details of Admission Test Fee / Processing Charges: Details about the Test
    Fee/Processing charges is available on the relevant pages in this Guide, Only Online
    payment mode is available for depositing the Test Fee/Processing charges. The details of
    online payment, if successful, will automatically be posted in the respective column of the
    Application Form. Candidates (or their parent/guardian in case of minors) are advised to
    ensure that their payment status is reflected on the application dashboard as well as on
    application PDF. Only those application where payment status is correctly reflected will only
    be deemed as successfully submitted.

```
Note: If the amount is deducted from candidate’s account but not reflected on
candidate’s application dashboard, then it will not be considered as successful
submission of application.
```
BASIC STEPS TO BE FOLLOWED IN ONLINE SUBMISSION OF APPLICATION FORM

Registering as a new user:

1. The candidate should register online and provide his / her correct and functional email
    because the username and password etc. will be sent on this email.
2. Please note every candidate will register separately and will get his/her username and
    password to access his/her Dashboard for filling as well as tracking the form(s).
3. Only Single Registration is sufficient for applying to the multiple courses by a candidate.

    to get the same on the registered email.

2. After saving the Profile, the candidate will be asked to review and confirm that the particulars
    entered are correct.
3. Candidate will not be able to Edit/Update his/her Profile after confirmation.
4. If a candidate finds any mistake in his/her Profile after confirmation, then he/she will have to
    re-register with different Username and Password to complete all the entries afresh.
